# Generic Magic Weapons


**See Also**:

- [Magic Items](Skyrim_Magic_Items.md): General information on magic items and how they appear
- [Weapons](Skyrim_Weapons.md): All of the basic weapons in the game
- [Staves](Skyrim_Staves.md): Staves are used for casting magical spells instead of physical attacks
- [Leveled Items](Skyrim_Leveled_Items.md): Leveled magic weapons, generally received as quest rewards
- [Unique Items](Skyrim_Unique_Items.md): Unique weapons, available from merchants or received as quest rewards
- [Artifacts](Skyrim_Artifacts.md): Unusually powerful one-of-a-kind weapons

## Improving Weapons
The statistics in the following tables are all base values, equivalent to the values for a player with 0 in all skills. Ways in which these statistics can be altered by your player's skills include:

- Increases in weapon skills ([One-handed](Skyrim_One-handed.md), [Two-handed](Skyrim_Two-handed.md), [Archery](Skyrim_Archery.md)) will automatically increase weapon damage. See [Weapons](Skyrim_Weapons.md) for details

- Tempering weapons at a [grindstone](Skyrim_Grindstone.md) will increase the weapon damage. - Tempering any magic weapon requires the [Arcane Blacksmith](Skyrim_Arcane_Blacksmith.md) perk to be unlocked. The type of ingot (or other material) necessary for the upgrade, as well as which [Smithing](Skyrim_Smithing.md) perk augments the upgrade, is the same as for the base version of the weapon. The base version of each weapon is highlighted via a link in the weapon name; that link leads to the page detailing the base weapon.

- The enchantment magnitude may be increased by perks in the appropriate magic school. For example, [Fire Damage](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage) enchantments are all increased by the [Destruction](Skyrim_Destruction.md) skill's [Augmented Flames](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Augmented_Flames) perk.

- The enchantment costs (listed in the "Charge/Cost = Uses" column) are affected by a relevant magic skill, as noted for each effect group. This means that the number of times an enchanted weapon can be used increases as your skill improves. At skill level 100 this results in about 1.7 times the uses documented here.

Unless noted otherwise, all of these items can be disenchanted.

## [Absorb Health](Skyrim_Absorb_Health.md)
Number of uses is increased by the [Destruction](Skyrim_Destruction.md) skill.

## [Chaos Damage](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Chaos_Damage)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
Number of uses is increased by the [Destruction](Skyrim_Destruction.md) skill.

The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Mod_Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.
